In addition to the above criteria, it is wished to be stated that attention was paid to the following specific criteria in respect of each application in granting the above licences.

1. Mr. N.U. Dissanayake, Lanka Filling

Station, Korasagolla.

i. High volume of vehicle traffic in the area.

ii. High population density and rapid

growth in other businesses.

iii. Satisfactory volume of sales on the

nearest filling station.

iv. Reporting of other infrastructure development and development plans in the area.

v. Strategic importance of the location.

vi. Compared to the limited space available in the nearest filling stations, this filling station being more spacious.

2. C.K.K. Seneviratne, Lanka Filling Station,

Galenbindunuwewa

i. Reports of high vehicle traffic in the area.

ii. High population density.

iii. Satisfactory sales capacity in filling

stations located close to this filling station.

iv. Reporting of other infrastructure development and development plans in the area.

v. The location being strategically important to the Ceylon Petroleum Corporation.

vi. The nearest filling station belonging to

the Corporation is 800 metres away from the location and is situated on a small plot of land 13.5 perches in extent and as such, cannot be further developed and the distance for other filling stations is at a satisfactory level.

3. Mr. W.G. Nandalal, Lanka Filling Station,

Kahatagasdigiliya

i. Reports of high vehicle traffic in the area.

ii. Reporting of other infrastructure development and development plans in the area.

iii. The location being strategically important to the Ceylon Petroleum Corporation.

iv. The location is by the A-12 highway

and fronting it.

v. Absence of filling stations nearby.

(The distance to Sippukulama filling station is 13 kilometres and the distance to W.G. Nandalal Filling Station is 22 kilometres.)

vi. Existence of a filling station of a

competitor company in the Kahatagasdigiliya Town and its failure to deliver services efficiently at times.

4. Mr. H.M.S. Jayaratne- Lanka Filling

Station, Bulnewa i. The relevant location is situated in predominantly agricultural area in Mahaweli H-Zone centred on the Bulnewa Town and it is an area of large-scale paddy cultivations. ii. Significant level of population density

with settlements associated with the Mahaweli Project. iii. The sales volumes of Galnewa filling

station and Thambuttegama filling station located 20 kilometres away being at a satisfactory level. iv. Reports of the implementation of

infrastructure development projects and development activities in nearby towns as the location is situated in Mahaweli H-Zone with many habitats. v. The location being strategically important for the operation of a filling station under the Ceylon Petroleum Corporation. vi. The location is situated on the left side

of B-501 road fronting the main road running from Thambuttegama to Galnewa.

5. Mr. A.W.W. Rohana Bandara, Lanka

Filling Station, Pubbogama

i. The location is situated on the right of Andiyagala-Madatugama B-556 road fronting the main road and this road and area is reported to be of high volume of vehicle traffic.

ii. The number of registered vehicles in

the area and the population density being high.

iii. The two nearest filling stations to this

filling station at Galnewa and Kekirawa are situated 27 kilometres and 15 kilometres away respectively and their sales volumes are at a satisfactory level to run a filling station at this location.

iv. The well-known “Namal Uyana”

forest reserve is situated in this area and implementation of infrastructure and other development projects.

v. The location being strategically important for the operation of a filling station under the Ceylon Petroleum Corporation.

6. Mr. K.K.D. Seneviratne, Lanka Filling

Station, Ikirigollewa

i. The location is situated in the right side along the Kandy-Jaffna A-9 road and it was reported that the area experiences a high traffic volume as vehicles travelling to Mannar, Vavuniya, Mullaitivu, Kilinochchi and Jaffna from various parts of the country are using this road.

ii. The filling stations at Rabewa, Mihintale and Medawachchiya which are the closest to the filling station have reported a satisfactory sales volumes for issuing a licence to this location.

iii. Renovations of the section of A-9 road

running across the area, cultivation activities of farmer habitats associated with Mahakanadarawa Tank and other infrastructure development and development activities of the Moragahakanda Project.

iv. As the location is situated by the A-9

road, the vehicles using the road can obtain a friendly and efficient service to the satisfaction of consumers from a CPC filling station and also the location being situated at a strategic place.

7. Mr. J. Thellanbura, Lanka Filling Station,

Sravastipura

i. The location is situated along A-028 Padeniya-Anuradhapura road at Thalawa with a distance of 7 kilometres towards Anuradhapura fronting the main road on the left side.

ii. High traffic volume being reported as a

large number of vehicles from many areas of the country use the A-028 road running opposite the filling station round the clock to travel to areas such as Anuradhapura, Mannar, Vavuniya, Mullaitivu, Kilinochchi and Jaffna.

iii. The location is at Nachchaduwa

Divisional Secretary's Division which has one of the highest population densities out of the 22 DS Divisions in the Anuradhapura District.

iv. The filling stations at Thalawa, Pothanegama and Anuradhapura which are the closest to the filling station have reported a satisfactory sales volume for issuing a licence to this location.

v. Reports of other infrastructure and

development projects being implemented in the area and accordingly an increase in fuel sales was expected during the implementation of these projects.

ගරු පරශක්ර සුමිත් ඳු වඹුර මන්ීුමා විසින් අසන ලද අද දින නයාය පත්‍රශේ 3වන ප්‍ර ්නයට - 2857/2023 - පිළිුර දීමට මුදල් ආර්ථික ස් ා උකරණ ස ජාතික ප්‍රතිපත්ති අමාතය ගරු රනිල් වික්‍රමසිං ම තා සති ශදකක කාලයක් ඉල්ලා ඇතර

ைொண்புைிகு யூ.ரக. சுைித் உடுகும்பு அெர்களொல் ரகட்கப் பட்ட இன்மறய ஒழுங்குப் பத்தி த்திலுள்ள 3ஆம் இலக்க ெினொவுக்கு - 2857/2023 - ெிமடயளிப்பதற்கு, ெிதி, தபொருளொதொ உறுதிப்பொடு ைற்றும் ரதசியக் தகொள்மககள் அமைச்சர் ைொண்புைிகு ணில் ெிக்கி ைசிங்ஹ அெர்கள் இ ண்டு ெொ கொல அெகொசம் ரகொொியுள்ளொர்.

The Hon. Ranil Wickremesinghe, Minister of Finance, Economic Stabilization and National Policies has requested for two weeks' time to reply to Question No. 3 - 2857/2023 - raised by the Hon. U. K. Sumith Udukumbura appearing in today’s Order Paper.

ඌව පළා් ක රජම ා ව ාරසරථාන සංරකෂණය

ஊெொ ைொகொணத்திலுள்ள ஜைஹொ ெிகொம கள்:

பொதுகொப்பு RAJAMAHA VIHARA TEMPLES IN UVA PROVINCE:

CONSERVATION

3647/2023 4. ගුණ වඩි්ේල් සු්ර්ෂර ම තා (ைொண்புைிகு ெடிரெல் சுர ஷ்) (The Hon. Vadivel Suresh)

ුේධ ාසන ආගමික ස සංස්කෘතික කටයුු අමාතයුමාශගන් ඇසූ ප්‍ර ්නය - (1):

(අ) (i) මුතියංගන රජම ා වි ාරය මියංගන රජම ා වි ාරය ස කතරගම ශේවාලය නව පළාත ුළ පිිටා තිශබන බවත්;

(ii) ආගමික ා සංස්කෘතික ැදියාවන් සිත සමාජයක් බිි කිරීම ඳශදසා බු ල්ල දිස්ත්‍රික්කය ඇුුව නව පළාත ුළ රජම ා වි ාරස් ාන රාශියක් පිිම්වා ඇති බවත්; රුමා දන්ශන්ද?

(ආ) (i) බු ල්ල දිස්ත්‍රික්කශේ ඇති රජම ා වි ාරස් ාන සංඛයාව ශකාපමණද;

(ii) ඒවාශේ නම් කවශර්ථද;

(iii) පුරාවිදයාව ා සම්බන්ධ පනත්වලට අනුූලලව රම රජම ා වි ාරස් ාන සංරක්ෂණය කරමින් පවතින්ශන්ද;

(iv) පස්සර ශබෝශගා ශදෝව මුතියංගන ස මියංගන රජම ා වි ාර ස අශන වත් රජම ා වි ාර සංරක්ෂණය කිරීම සඳ ා ශම් දක්වා ශගන ඇති ක්‍රියාමාර්ථග කවශර්ථද;

යන්න රුමා ශමම සභාවට දන්වන්ශන්ද?

1365 1366

[ගරු කං න විශජ්ශස්කර ම තා]

2023 කක්ශතෝබර්ථ 20

(ඇ) (i) ශබෞේධ ජනතාවශේ ආගමික සංස්කෘතික වටපිටාවට අනුූලලව ස ඓති ාසික ඳරුමය සුරක්ිත වන පරිදි ඉ ත සංරක්ෂණ කටයුු කිරීමට පියවර ශගන තිශේද;

(ii) ශමම ඓති ාසික ආගමික ඳරුමයන් අනාගත පරම්පරාශේ ප්‍රශයෝජනය සඳ ා සුරක්ිත කිරීමට ගනු ලබන ක්‍රියාමාර්ථග කවශර්ථද;

යන්නත් රුමා ශමම සභාවට දන්වන්ශන්ද?

(ඈ) ශනාරශස් නම් ඒ මන්ද? புத்தசொசன, சைய ைற்றும் கலொசொ அலுெல்கள் அமைச் சம க் ரகட்ட ெினொ:

(அ) (i) முத்தியங்கமன ஜைஹொ ெிகொம , ைஹியங் கமன ஜைஹொ ெிகொம ைற்றும் கதிர்கொைக் ரகொயில் என்பமெ ஊெொ ைொகொணத்தில் அமைந்துள்ளன என்பமதயும்;

(ii) சைய ைற்றும் கலொசொ ெிழுைியங்களுடன்கூடிய சமூகதைொன்மற உருெொக்கும் ரெொக்கில், பதுமள ைொெட்டம் உட்பட ஊெொ ைொகொணத்தில் பல ஜைஹொ ெிகொம கள் அமைக்கப் பட்டுள்ளன என்பமதயும்;

அெர் அறிெொ ொ?

(ஆ) (i) பதுமள ைொெட்டத்தில் அமைந்துள்ள ஜைஹொ ெிகொம களின் எண்ணிக்மக யொததன்பமதயும்;

(ii) அெற்றின் தபயர்கள் யொமெதயன்பமதயும்;

(iii) ததொல்தபொருள் சட்டங்களுக்கு அமைெொக ரைற்படி ஜைஹொ ெிகொம கள் ரபணிப் பொதுகொக்கப்பட்டு ெருகின்றனெொ என்பமதயும்;

(iv) பசமற, ரபொதகொமட, ரதொெ, முத்தியங்கமன ைற்றும் ைஹியங்கமன ஜைஹொ ெிகொம கமள யும் ஏமனய ஜைஹொ ெிகொம கமளயும் ரபணிப் பொதுகொப்பதற்கொக இதுெம ரைற் தகொள்ளப்பட்டுள்ள ெடெடிக்மககள் யொமெ தயன்பமதயும்; அெர் இச்சமபக்கு அறிெிப்பொ ொ?

(இ) (i) தபௌத்த ைக்களுமடய சைய, கலொசொ பின்னணிக்கமைெொகவும், ெ லொற்றுச் சிறப்பு ைிக்க ை புொிமைமயப் பொதுகொக்கும் ெமகயிலும், ரைற்படி ரபணல் ெடெடிக்மககமள ரைற் தகொள்ெதற்கொன ெடெடிக்மககள் ரைற்தகொள் ளப்பட்டுள்ளனெொ என்பமதயும்;

(ii) இந்த ெ லொற்றுச் சிறப்புைிக்க ை புொிமைகமள எதிர்கொலச் சந்ததியினொின் ெலன்கருதிப் பொது கொப்பதற்கொக ரைற்தகொள்ளப்படும் ெடெடிக் மககள் யொமெதயன்பமதயும்;

அெர் இச்சமபக்கு அறிெிப்பொ ொ?

(ஈ) இன்ரறல், ஏன்?

asked the Minister of Buddhasasana, Religious and Cultural Affairs:

(a) Is he aware that -

(i) the Muthiyangana Rajamaha Viharaya, Mahiyangana Rajamaha Viharaya and Kataragama Devalaya are located in the Uva Province; and

(ii) many Rajamaha Vihara temples have been established in Uva Province including Badulla District in order to create a society with religious and cultural values?

(b) Will he inform this House -

(i) the number of RajamahaVihara temples in Badulla District;

(ii) their names;

(iii) whether the aforesaid Rajamaha Vihara temples are being conserved in accordance with the related archaeological acts; and

(iv) the steps hitherto taken to preserve the Rajamaha Viharas of Passara, Bogoda, Dowa, Muthiyangana and Mahiyangana and other Rajamaha Viharas?

(c) Will he also inform this House -

(i) whether measures have been taken to carry out the above conservation activities in accordance with the religious and cultural environment of the Buddhists while protecting the historical heritage; and

(ii) the measures that will be taken to secure these historical religious heritages for the benefit of the future generation?

(d) If not, why?

ගුණ වදු ර වක්‍රමනායක ම තා (ුේධාශාසන, ආගමික ස සංසරකෘතික ක යුුර අමාතයුරමා) (ைொண்புைிகு ெிதுற ெிக்கி ைெொயக்க - புத்தசொசன, சைய ைற்றும் கலொசொ அலுெல்கள் அமைச்சர்) (The Hon. Vidura Wickramanayaka - Minister of Buddhasasana, Religious and Cultural Affairs)

(අ) (i) කේර

(ii) කේර

(ආ) (i) 84යිර

(ii) ඇමුුම 01හි* දැක්ශේර

(iii) වි ාරස් ාන සංරක්ෂණය සඳ ා ඒ ඒ වි ාරස් ානවල සාම්ප්‍රදායානුූලලව පැවතශගන රන ක්‍රමයන් සඳ ා ස ශයෝගය දැක්ීම සිු ශේර රිදී පුරාවිදයා අණ පනත්වලට ා සංරක්ෂණ ප්‍රතිපත්තිවලට පට ැනි ශනාවන ආකාරයට පුරාවිදයා ශදපාර්ථතශම්න්ුශේ ඳපශදස් ා නිරන්තර අධීක්ෂණය යටශත් සංරක්ෂණ කටයුු සිු ශේර මූලය ප්‍රතිපාදන ශ ෝ රවය අදාළ වි ාරස් ානය මඟින් සම්පාදනය කරනු ලබන අතර ශ්‍රම දායකත්වය පුරාවිදයා ශදපාර්ථතශම්න්ුව මඟින් සපයනු ලැශේර

මීට අමතරව පුරාවිදයා ශදපාර්ථතශම්න්ුව මඟින් සංරක්ෂණ අව යතා ඇති ස්මාරක ඳුනා ගනිමින් ඒ ඒ ස්මාරකයන් සඳ ා ඍජුවම මැදි ත් ශවමින් මධයම රජය මඟින් ලබා ශදන ප්‍රතිපාදනයන්ට

පාර්ථලිශම්න්ුව

අනුූලලව පුරාවිදයා අණ පනත්වලට ා සංරක්ෂණ ප්‍රතිපත්තිවලට අනුූලලව සංරක්ෂණ කටයුු සිු කරනු ලැශේර

(iv) ඇමුුම 02හි* දැක්ශේර

(ඇ) (i) කේර

(ii) පුරාවිදයා අණ පනත්වලට ා සංරක්ෂණ ප්‍රතිපත්තිවලට පට ැනි ශනාවන ආකාරයට පුරාවිදයා ශදපාර්ථතශම්න්ු ඳපශදස් ා නිරන්තර අධීක්ෂණය යටශත් සංරක්ෂණය කරමින් ශමම ශලති ාසික ආගමික ඳරුමයන් අනාගත පරම්පරාශේ ප්‍රශයෝජනය සඳ ා සුරක්ිත කිරීම සිු කරනු ලබයිර

(ඈ) අදාළ ශනාශේර

(அ) (i) ஆம்.

(ii) ஆம்.

(ஆ) (i) 84

(ii) இமணப்பு 01*இல் குறிப்பிடப்பட்டுள்ளது.

(iii) ெிகொம கமளப் பொதுகொக்க, அந்தந்த ெிகொம

களின் பொ ம்பொிய சடங்குகமள ஆதொிக்க ரெண்டியது அெசியைொகும். அங்கு ததொல்லியல் திமணக்களத்தின் ெழிகொட்டுதல் ைற்றும் ததொடர் கண்கொணிப்பின்கீழ், ததொல்லியல் ெிதிகள் ைற்றும் பொதுகொப்புக் ரகொட்பொடுகளுக்கு மு ணொக இல்லொத ெமகயில், பொதுகொப்பு ெடெடிக்மககள் ரைற்தகொள்ளப்படுகின்றன. ெிதி ஒதுக்கீடு அல்லது அெற்றுக்கொன தபொருட்கள் அந்தந்த ெிகொம யொல் ெழங்கப்படுெதுடன், ததொல்லியல் திமணக்களம்மூலம் ததொழிலொளர் பங்களிப்பும் ெழங்கப்படும்.

ரைலும், ததொல்லியல் திமணக்களைொனது, பொதுகொப்பு ரதமெப்படும் ெிமனவுச் சின்னங் கமளக் கண்டறிந்து, ைத்திய அ சு ெிதித்துள்ள ெிதிகளின்படி, அந்தந்த ெிமனவுச் சின்னங் களின் ெிடயத்தில் ரெ டியொகத் தமலயிட்டு, ததொல்லியல் சட்டங்கள் ைற்றும் பொதுகொப்பு ெிதிமுமறகளின்படி, பொதுகொப்பு ெடெடிக்மக கமள ரைற்தகொள்கின்றன.

(iv) இமணப்பு 02* இல் குறிப்பிடப்பட்டுள்ளது.

(இ) (i) ஆம்.

(ii) ததொல்லியல் திமணக்களத்தின் ஆரலொசமன ைற்றும் ததொடர் கண்கொணிப்பின்கீழ், ததொல்லி யல் ெிதிகள் ைற்றும் பொதுகொப்புக் ரகொட்பொடு களுக்கு மு ணொக இல்லொத ெமகயில், ெருங்கொல சந்ததியினொின் பயன்பொட்டிற்கொக இந்த ெ லொற்று சைய ை புகள் பொதுகொக்கப்பட்டு ெரு கின்றன.

(ஈ) தபொருத்தைற்றது.

(a) (i) Yes.

(ii) Yes.

(b) (i) 84.

(ii) Given in Annex-01*.

(iii) Cooperation is provided for traditional methods of the respective temples for the conservation of temples. The conservation works are carried out under the instructions and continuous supervision of the Department of Archaeology without contravening archaeological ordinances and conservation policies. The financial provision or material is provided by the relevant temple and the labour contribution is provided by the Department of Archaeology.

In addition to this, the Department of Archaeology identifies the monuments in need of conservation and intervenes directly for the respective monuments in accordance with the allocation provided by the Central Government and conservation activities are carried out in accordance with the archaeological ordinances and conservation policies.

(iv) Given in Annex-02*

(c) (i) Yes.

(ii) These historic religious heritages are being conserved for the benefit of future generation by conserving them under the instructions and continuous supervision of the Department of Archaeology without contravening archaeological ordinances and conservation policies.

(d) Not relevant.

ගරු (ආ ාර්ථය) රිනි අමරසූරිය මන්ීුමිය විසින් අසන ලද අද දින නයාය පත්‍රශේ සඳ න් 5වන ප්‍ර ්නයට - 3678/2023 - පිළිුර දීමට අධයාපන අමාතය ගරු (ආ ාර්ථය) සුසිල් ශේමජයන්ත ම තා සති ශදකක කාලයක් ඉල්ලා ඇතර

ைொண்புைிகு (கலொெிதி) (தசல்ெி) ஹொினி அை சூொிய அெர்களொல் ரகட்கப்பட்ட இன்மறய ஒழுங்குப் பத்தி த்திலுள்ள 5ஆம் இலக்க ெினொவுக்கு - 3678/2023 - ெிமடயளிப்பதற்கு, கல்ெி அமைச்சர் ைொண்புைிகு (கலொெிதி) சுசில் பிர ைஜயந்த அெர்கள் இ ண்டு ெொ கொல அெகொசம் ரகொொியுள்ளொர்.

The Hon. (Dr.) Susil Premajayantha, Minister of Education has requested for two weeks' time to reply to Question No. 5 - 3678/2023 - raised by the Hon. (Dr.) (Ms.) Harini Amarasuriya appearing in today’s Order Paper.

[ගරු විු ර වික්‍රමනායක ම තා]

————————— * පුසරතකාල්ේ තබා ඇත. * நூனிமலயத்தில் மெக்கப்பட்டுள்ளது. * Placed in the Library.

සැ.යු.

ශමම වාර්ථතාශේ අවසාන මුරණය සඳ ා ස්වකීය නිවැරදි කළ යුු තැන් දක්වනු රිසි මන්ීන් මින් පිටපතක් ශගන නිවැරදි කළ යුු ආකාරය රි පැ ැදිලිව ල වණු ශකාට පිටපත ලැමට ශදසතියක් ශනාඉක්මවා ැන්සාේ සංස්කාරක ශවත ලැශබන ශස් රවිය යුුයර

குறிப்பு

உறுப்பினர் இறுதிப் பதிப்பிற் தசய்யெிரும்பும் பிமழ திருத்தங்கமளத் தைது பி தியில் ததளிெொகக் குறித்து அதமனப் பிமழ

திருத்தப்படொத பி தி கிமடத்த இரு ெொ ங்களுள் ஹன்சொட் பதிப்பொசிொியருக்கு அனுப்புதல் ரெண்டும்.

රජ්ේ ප්‍රවෘ කති ්දපාර්ත්පන්ුර්ේ ිළහිටි රජ්ේ ප්‍රකාශන කාර්යාංශ්යන්

බාගත ැක.

ஹன்சொட் அறிக்மகயின் பி திகமள இல. 163, கிருலப்பமன வீதி, தபொல்ரஹன்தகொட, தகொழும்பு 5இல் அமைந்துள்ள

அ சொங்க தகெல் திமணக்களத்தின் அ சொங்க தெளியீடுகள் அலுெலகத்தில்

பணம் தசலுத்திப் தபற்றுக்தகொள்ளலொம்.
